< text>
I'm not sure why this place has such high reviews, since my experience (and especially the service) was very mediocre.

We didn't really know what the concept was for this place (order smaller dishes and share, or order something bigger per person?) so we specifically asked one of the waiters about that, and the only thing he could tell us was that "everything on the menu is the best". Five minutes later we asked again for the best dishes on the menu, but this time another waiter, and again the response we received was "everything on the menu tastes good".

I mean... are you kidding me? Can't even the staff who works there help us out with what to order?

In the end we played it safe by ordering the half chicken and the taco's, and however they tasted fine, it was by no means something special. Not a place I would go again myself next time.</text>

<Date>1487506650985</Date><GmapID>0x808f7fb99420ca19:0xc3f1dfd1082c100c< /GmapID><review>One of several relatively new hipster-flavored restaurants in Dogpatch, Gilberth's is a little cheaper and a little better (in every regard) than some other options like Serpentine. I'm not particularly fond of this type of restaurant, but if you have a group of friends who are into it, this is one of your better options in the area. It's still spendy, but most everything new is, and there are some genuinely tasty items on the menu. <user>114011040269846758599< /user><name>P Y< /name>< date>
1466254858423< /date>
<Rate>5</Rate>< review>
Must have been a fairly new establishment because I have never seen or noticed it in the Dogpatch area. I was yelping for dinner places to go to and this popped up. I'm glad I chose this place, because all the dishes I tried here are awesome. They have plenty of bottled beer and wine options. As for food, the pulled pork was really teally really satisfying. It came with a few sides of crispy plantains that were very crunchy and delicious. The next dish was the suckling pig which was also very delicious,  but personally I like the pulled pork i.e. Cubano dish, the most. Very yummy. I also tried the churros for dessert and loved it. I went here for dinner right as they opened at 17:30, so there was no wait and the waiters were all very nice and attentive. I would come back and would love to try their other dishes some time in the near future! :)
P.S. this review is for their dinner serving.  I have never tried their brunch or lunch menu.<//review>

< Review>
Josh was pouring for us when I visited recently with a chef from NYC and a friend from Napa, wow, awesome wine. Love Jada's wines and we found everyone at the winery are so accommodating, knowledgeable and friendly. Since my visit I recommend friends and people visiting from outside the area to their tasting room. The drive there is also spectacular. It is located on the most beautiful westside area of Paso Robles Wine Country.

Hell's Kitchen is one of my favorites although all of their other Rhone and Bordeaux style wines are a real treat too that Wine Enthusiast and Wine Spectator have rated high.

Icing on the cake is that they use biodaynamic practices making them 100% sustainably farmed!

Everything to love!<//Review>

We quickly pulled off on the side of the road to discover the chains had been sparking because they had apparently been dragging across the road. Luckily, we made it home in one piece.
